            <div class="main section" id="main">
             <div class="widget Blog" id="Blog1">
              <div class="blog-posts hfeed">
               <!-- google_ad_section_start(name=default) -->
               <div class="date-outer">
                <h2 class="date-header">
                 <span>
                  Oct 6, 2013
                 </span>
                </h2>
                <div class="date-posts">
                 <div class="post-outer">
                  <div class="post hentry">
                   <a name="3229528616080299322">
                   </a>
                   <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
                    <a href="http://www.skinnytaste.com/2013/10/whole-grain-apple-nut-muffins.html">
                     Whole Grain Apple Nut Muffins
                    </a>
                   </h3>
                   <div class="post-header" style="width:100%;">
                    <div style="float:left; margin:0 12px 0 0;">
                     <div>
                      <script>
                       (function(d){
                                                var js, id = 'facebook-jssdk'; if (d.getElementById(id)) {return;}
                                                js = d.createElement('script'); js.id = id; js.async = true;
                                                                     js.src = "//connect.facebook.net/en_US/all.js#xfbml=1";
                                                                     d.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].appendChild(js);
                                                                     }
                                                                     (document));
                      </script>
                      <fb:like action="like" colorscheme="light" font="arial" href="http://www.skinnytaste.com/2013/10/whole-grain-apple-nut-muffins.html" layout="button_count" send="false" show_faces="false">
                      </fb:like>
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div style="float:left; margin:0;">
                     <a class="twitter-share-button" data-count="horizontal" data-lang="en" data-related="skinnytaste:SkinnyTaste Recipes" data-text="Whole Grain Apple Nut Muffins" data-url="http://www.skinnytaste.com/2013/10/whole-grain-apple-nut-muffins.html" data-via="skinnytaste" href="http://twitter.com/share" rel="nofollow">
                     </a>
                    </div>
                    <div style="float:left; margin:0 0 0 -14px">
                     <su:badge layout="1" location="http://www.skinnytaste.com/2013/10/whole-grain-apple-nut-muffins.html">
                     </su:badge>
                    </div>
                    <div class="post-comment-link" style="float:right; margin:auto;">
                    </div>
                    <br style="clear:both;"/>
                   </div>
                   <div class="post-body entry-content">
                    <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                     <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-XeqTWCKbAjA/UlF_lwnHK8I/AAAAAAAAMJ4/osnEP64e1K8/s1600/Whole-Grain-Apple-Muffins.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                      <img border="0" class="pinnable" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-XeqTWCKbAjA/UlF_lwnHK8I/AAAAAAAAMJ4/osnEP64e1K8/s1600/Whole-Grain-Apple-Muffins.jpg"/>
                     </a>
                    </div>
                    <br/>
                    Whole grain apple muffins made with fresh apple, applesauce, walnuts plus a combination of bran flour, white whole wheat and almond meal with a granola topping.
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    It's apple season and I picked up some gala apples at the farmer's market last week to make a great big batch of
                    <a href="http://www.skinnytaste.com/2011/10/crock-pot-applesauce.html">
                     crock pot applesauce
                    </a>
                    . Last year I used that applesauce to make an
                    <a href="http://www.skinnytaste.com/2011/10/applesauce-nut-bread.html">
                     applesauce nut bread
                    </a>
                    which I love, and it inspired me to experiment with almond meal, wheat bran and flax to come up with these delicious muffins. I love how moist they turned out, and I saved the extra in my refrigerator to eat for the week  they stayed moist for days!
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    <a name="more">
                    </a>
                    <br/>
                    <b>
                     Whole Grain Apple Nut Muffins
                    </b>
                    <br/>
                    <span style="font-size: x-small;">
                     <i>
                      Skinnytaste.com
                     </i>
                    </span>
                    <br/>
                    Servings: 12  Size: 1 muffin  Old Points: 3 pts  Points+: 4 pts
                    <br/>
                    Calories: 149  Fat: 5 g  Carb: 30 g  Fiber: 4 g  Protein: 4 g  Sugar: 19 g
                    <br/>
                    Sodium: 172 mg  Cholesterol: 0 g
                    <b>
                    </b>
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    Ingredients:
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    <ul>
                     <li>
                      1 cup (from 1 large) apple, peeled cored and grated
                     </li>
                     <li>
                      1/4 tsp + 1/2 tsp cinnamon
                     </li>
                     <li>
                      1 tbsp honey
                     </li>
                     <li>
                      1/2 tsp lemon juice
                     </li>
                     <li>
                      cooking spray
                     </li>
                     <li>
                      3/4 cups King Arthur white whole wheat flour
                     </li>
                     <li>
                      3/4 cup coarse wheat bran flour
                     </li>
                     <li>
                      1/4 cup almond meal
                     </li>
                     <li>
                      1 tsp baking soda
                     </li>
                     <li>
                      1/8 tsp ground nutmeg
                     </li>
                     <li>
                      1/4 tsp salt
                     </li>
                     <li>
                      1 1/2 tbsp ground flaxseeds
                     </li>
                     <li>
                      1 1/2 cups
                      <a href="http://www.skinnytaste.com/2011/10/crock-pot-applesauce.html">
                       homemade applesauce
                      </a>
                      (or store bought)
                     </li>
                     <li>
                      3/4 cup brown sugar, not packed
                     </li>
                     <li>
                      1 tbsp coconut oil (or canola)
                     </li>
                     <li>
                      2 large egg whites
                     </li>
                     <li>
                      2 tsp vanilla extract
                     </li>
                     <li>
                      1 oz walnuts, chopped
                     </li>
                     <li>
                      1 oz granola (I used Cascadian Farms)
                     </li>
                    </ul>
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    Directions:
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    In a medium bowl combine grated apple, 1/4 tsp cinnamon, honey, and lemon juice. Set aside.
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                     <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/--L-qod0qyhc/UlF_oAtx_7I/AAAAAAAAMKM/vDkh8HSygmo/s1600/grated-apple.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                      <img border="0" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/--L-qod0qyhc/UlF_oAtx_7I/AAAAAAAAMKM/vDkh8HSygmo/s1600/grated-apple.jpg"/>
                     </a>
                    </div>
                    <br/>
                    Preheat oven to 350F. Line a muffin tin with liners and lightly spray them with cooking spray.
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    In a medium bowl, combine flour, bran, almond meal, flax, baking soda, nutmeg, cinnamon, and salt with a wire whisk; set aside.
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    In a large bowl mix applesauce, coconut oil, egg whites, sugar, and vanilla; beat at medium speed until thick. Scrape down sides of the bowl.
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    Add the flour mixture, then blend at low speed until combined. Do not over mix. Fold in apples and walnuts.
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                     <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-nQONxDIhf7o/UlF_l2VHFCI/AAAAAAAAMJ8/sucYFVQj32Q/s1600/Whole-Grain-Apple-Muffin.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                      <img border="0" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-nQONxDIhf7o/UlF_l2VHFCI/AAAAAAAAMJ8/sucYFVQj32Q/s1600/Whole-Grain-Apple-Muffin.jpg"/>
                     </a>
                    </div>
                    <br/>
                    Pour batter into muffin tins and top each muffin with 1/2 teaspoon of granola, then bake in the center rack about 35 minutes, or until a toothpick inserted in the center comes out clean.
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    Let them cool and serve room temperature.
                    <div style="clear: both;">
                    </div>
